String.prototype.matchAll() - JavaScript | MDN
https://developer.mozilla.org/zh-CN/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/String/matchAll

const regexp = /t(e)(st(\d?))/g;
const str = 'test1test2';

const array = [...str.matchAll(regexp)];

console.log(array[0]);
// Expected output: Array ["test1", "e", "st1", "1"]

console.log(array[1]);
// Expected output: Array ["test2", "e", "st2", "2"]

ã€€6//sp1it=1ã€€6//?â­=3ã€€&when=2023/10/4 17:46:33ã€€&!=ğŸ›‘ã€€&visible=1
JavaScript speech synthesis cheatsheet
https://devhints.io/js-speech

function speak (message) {
  var msg = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(message)
  var voices = window.speechSynthesis.getVoices()
  msg.voice = voices[0]
  window.speechSynthesis.speak(msg)
}
speak('Hello, world')
